< text>
Union City isn't my usual stomping ground but I was in the area with a few hours to kill and an unruly mop of hair on my head. D&R popped up on my search and I decided to take a chance. Boy am I glad I did. I didn't have an appointment so I had to wait about 30 minutes but the haircut and friendly service was well worth the wait. I ended up with Jeremy (second chair from the door on the right) and he did a fantastic job.  I might have to accidentally end up in Union City again in about 6-8 week. Tips: make an appointment and bring cash.< /text>

I've gone to this Acapulco a few times. I mostly go when it's around my birthday because I'm signed up for their e-club and get a free meal. The service is usually up to par, nothing extraordinary. The food comes out in a decent amount of time, always hot. I like how they taste better than any and all El Toritos I've been to and yet they're owned by the same company. They're a bit slow with refilling the chips and salsa and drinks--but it's never a huge issue. I always go there when it's not crowded. The last time I went, when I showed my server the voucher for my free birthday meal, she had to give it to the manager. He came to my table and asked me if it was my birthday, I told him it passed but was still celebrating it. He was really nice and joked around with me. Later on, I'm waiting for confirmation that everything was good and they came singing happy birthday to me and also gave me free flan. I was not expecting that and was completely embarrassed, but it was a nice gesture.</Review>

<gmapID>0x80c2c6357a71e59b:0xb2930b6a7cb869f8< /gmapID>< review>
I would like to propose a toast: to the best cocktail bar in Downtown Los Angeles.

The nondescript entrance whose only demarcation is a lion door knocker gives this bar a members-only private club feel.  But, the symbolism of the brass lion is not one of isolation and exclusivity, rather of power and strength - like the cocktails they pour.

The interior is dark.  With the limited sense of sight, come the heightened senses of smell and taste - making you acutely aware that what you are drinking is a perfectly balanced cocktail, one made with the freshest of ingredients and quality of spirits.

The Association is where I fell in love with 99 year old New Yorker - The French 75, part gin, part champagne.  They just don't make them like they use to and no one makes it like The Association.

May they continue to pour balanced.<//review>

<name>JR C<//name><Text>The Low-Down=-- Friday Night, No Cover, Poppin, Dark!

Rolled into The Association on a Friday Night and this place is packed, but fortunately there was not a line at the door. The entrance is unmarked and the bar is unlabeled, but know that the entrance to this place is a big solid door and shares the same depressed stairways as Cole's.

Inside was pretty poppin, but this place could be the darkest bar I've ever been in. So dark that your hand would disappear if you stretch it out in front of you. Regardless, there was a crowded cushy seating area which took up about half this place, and the other half would be a standing room that surrounded the single bar. It wasn't dancy, booty-bass music that was playing, and it wasn't too loud either, because I could remember having conversations, and actually remembering what I heard.

Once I made it through the crowd to the bar, it was not long before I was helped, so big plus for that. The bartenders paid a lot of attention to their drinks, but the price also reflected with an average of 11 to 12 bucks per drink. I tried the New York Sour, and it was not too shabby with plenty of stiffness. There were other specialty drinks that I'd probably have to try here.<//Text>< Rate>

<userid>105092658195117649597</userid>< Name>

<Time>1421351920166< /Time><rating>4< /rating><Review>Saturday Night Review

10pm-No line,11pm-Line-----Good thing the door man remembered me from earlier and let me skip right into the place, yay! It pays to be a girl sometimes, right ladies?!  The location is a little hard to find if you've never been there; it's on 6th street, just east of Main on the south side. Make sense??? *laughs* Just look for the depressed stairways!

Be warn, this place is daaark! I couldn't even see anything when I first stepped in. It took me about a good 5 minutes before my eyes adjusted.  The place was packed with a diverse crowds and electro music popping in the background. The place is small, but it has plenty of seating for ladies with weary feet. They have a long bar with about 3-4 bartenders working that night....Matthew was my bartender for the night and he made my drinks quite stiff in a good way! Although he picked on me, I really liked him cause he reminded me of an old crush that did the same thing. Plus, he made my drinks extra delicious!

Tonight, I tried the Pisco Sour (Pisco, lime juice, simple syrup, & 1 egg white with a dash of bitter.) and the Indian Summer. Both were delicious! I love any drinks with egg white as part of the ingredients because it gives an extra frothiness. Get it if you're a fan like me! If you want something refreshing that's similar to your favorite liquor with soda, get the Indian Summer! It was light and tasty with a hint of grapefruit in it. The only downfall is that the Indian Summer is so easy to drink that it'll go as fast as your water, except you'll be super buzz!

Can't wait to come back for their Happy Hour! (Mon-Fri 5pm-10pm with their specialty drinks for $5)</Review><Pics>None< /Pics>< resp>
None<//resp>

<user>105624405058336158396<//user><name>Jeff Nash< /name><Time>1555071557685< /Time><rating>5<//rating>< text>
This is NOT the nearest laundromat to my place of business, but I prefer to drive a few extra miles and utilize this well-managed business.
There are single- and multi-load washing machines.  And all of them appear clean, well-maintained, and fully functional.
There are two walls of dryers which provide 8 minutes of drying time for 25 cents (true as of April 2019).  Other laundromats in the vicinity give 4 minutes for 25 cents.
There are lots of square feet of laundry folding counter-top surface.
The staff is cheerful and friendly.  There are laundry products for sale in the office, although I'm not sure what time that opens or closes.  I know it's not open when the laundry opens at 6:00 AM.
There is a soda machine, a snack machine, and a video game for those with extra quarters.
The other customers are polite while also keeping to themselves.  But I recommend avoiding on Sunday's - those sweet little abuelas can be a bit territorial about which machines , baskets, and laundry folding surfaces they prefer.</text>

<Date>1541601886849< /Date>< Rating>
5</Rating>
< text>
I am not a fan of airport services, including restaurants.  My dislike is not only the inflated prices, but is overshadowed but the robotic service and lack of personal touch. I was pleasantly suprised during my recent flight out of this San Jose airport.  I had a breakfast while I waited for boarding. The food was good and well worth the price.

What really supprised me was the service. Eye contact, smiles and a feeling of genuine concern that I enjoyed the meal. The staff had the kind of attitude Disney would be proud of. As a whole, the meal and restaurant  earned a very good rating. I am not one to give praise for expected behavior. I feel this story should be told.

Of special interest was what happened after I walked out and to my gate. When at my gate I realized I left my book at the restaurant.  I walked back to the restaurant hoping for what I thought would be the best, the book would be behind the bar or somewhere they put forgotten articles. To my surprise the staff recognized me and told me my server  Francisco, had run to my gate and taken my book to return it to me. I must have passed him on the way back to the restaurant.  To add to the event, I was using boarding passes from a trip of months ago as a bookmark. When Francisco went to the wrong gate, as listed on the boarding pass, he could have given up. He did not. When I returned to the gate I was to fly out of, there he was. Through detective work, he had found me.

I told him, I could not believe he had taken the time to return my book. His replay was I was still his guest. Get that, an airport restaurant staff with a customer service attitude of a four star establishment. Either Francisco is an isolated anomaly  or the result of effective management. Judging by the rest of the staff, it is either good management or Francisco has an infectious customer service attitude.

I would ask my fellow travelers, passing through the San Jose airport, stop In to the Tres Gringos restaraunt and enjoy a meal. If given the opportunity, tip well
They deserve it!</text>

< Text>
I don't even know where to start, but if you're reading this and care about yourself GO SOMEWHERE ELSE!

I had to wait over 30 mins and then literally beg to get a freaking glass of water because the waiter didn't even bother to stop and say, "Hey I'll be with you". So we got a bottled drink when he took our order, and again, I had to get up to go get it myself because he forgot.

Finally when we got our Cheese quesadilla, the food tasted like Mission Tortillas and Great Value Mexican three cheese blend and they wanted to charge 25 for our ticket.

I called over the manager to tell her that the food taste really bad and you know what she tells me? That maybe I just never had that type of cheese quesadilla before. Um, I'm Mexican, I've had every type of cheese quesadilla you can think of and they don't taste this crappy.

After sitting there defending her food and establishment like something off of Kitchen Nightmares, she finally decided to try and fix the situation by just not charging us for the food.

Summed up we spent almost an hour and didn't even eat.

Seriously I spent those 25$ at the freaking convenience store at the airport on nuts and water and it was a better meal than what they tried to serve me.

STAY AWAY I promise you'll regret it.</Text>

<time>1495912823874< /time>< Review>
The trails and wide sidewalks are good for young bikers and multiples strollers, and the playground promotes a diverse amount of play ability. My son could climb the easy way up and slide down the slide to me at 18 mo, and his sister still enjoys testing her climbing and bars abilities as a teen-ager. The field on the other side of the trail is perfect for playing Frisbee or ball or tag, or flying a kite, or just running around. There are bathrooms and water fountains, even one for your pets. Two picnic tables, several tennis courts, shade trees spaced nicely. All contained in a small space in a way that feels wide open.</Review>

< Text>
Several years ago, I started using a CPAP machine. My medical group only contracts with Apria Healthcare for durable medical equipment, which was my first encounter with the company. They ended up overcharging me for the machine and supplies.

When I called them to point out their error, they acted like they didn‚Äôt know what I was talking about. I had to go to Apria‚Äôs offices and explain the mistake to the person that wrote up the order. Finally convinced them they overcharged me, and they agreed to send me a refund check. Weeks went by, and when the check finally arrived, it was for far less than the overcharged amount. I called them back and through the whole scenario again. Weeks later, another check came; it was also less than the amount they owed.

Once again, I called and explained the situation, and again, they agreed to send a refund check. Weeks later, the check arrived and was for the correct final amount they owed me.  It took multiple phone calls, a trip to Apria‚Äôs offices, and over three months to get my money back.

In early December of 2020, I was having problems with my CPAP mask. My doctor recommended a new mask style and gave me a sample in a small size that I ended up not using because it was too small. I called Apria to check  the cost for that style of mask in the medium size because I know there are many things that I can buy on the open market (same manufacturer and model) for what my copay would be or less). The Apria rep told me they needed a prescription before telling me what the cost would be. I had the doctor send Apria the prescription, and I called Apria back. I was then told they had to enter the order before telling me what the cost was. I said, fine, since I knew I could cancel the order before giving them the payment information.

The rep told me there would be NO out-of-pocket cost for me. I was surprised because I understood there could be a 20% copay. I reverified with the rep three times there would be no out-of-pocket cost for me for the mask and told the rep each time I wanted to make sure what he was telling me was accurate because if there were an out-of-pocket cost for me, I would not place the order. The rep assured me each time, the system said there was no copay, so I ordered the mask.

The mask took about a month to arrive, and today I received a bill for the copay. I called Apria again but was informed the bill was a legitimate charge because the insurance company did not pay the total amount.  I don‚Äôt think it‚Äôs a fair charge because if I had been given accurate information and not lied to, I would not have placed the order. I asked to talk to the supervisor but was told the supervisor was busy with another customer but would call me back. I never did get that call.

Based on my experiences, I believe Apria has the shadiest, crookedest business practices of any company I have ever dealt with.

UPDATE: I received a call from an Apria Billing Specialist this morning. She acknowledged Apria owned the problem and addressed it by issuing a credit to my account for the billed amount.<//Text>

< text>
I wish I would have seen these reviews before I ever worked with this company.  My doctor referred me to Apria for a CPAP machine.  They contacted me and asked for a deposit of about $80 so they could send the machine out.  I paid it over the phone.  There was no mention of any other possible charges - in fact, they specifically stated that deposit was the only thing I had to pay.  I got the machine and it just doesn't work for me.  I called to ask how to return but due to covid, the representative was working from home and told me someone would call me back.  I got emails from them saying my machine wasn't transmitting data.  No mention of money, nothing in the mail.  No documents in the box that the machine came in.

A few weeks later I notice a charge on my bank account from Apria.  $13, so no big deal, but I didn't understand why or how they could charge me again.  I didn't authorize automatic payment.  Before I even had the chance to call and ask about it, another charge shows up on my bank account for $54.  This time I call immediately and they claim they can't reverse it until it officially posts to my account, as it was "pending" when I called.  They agreed they shouldn't have charged me and did not have authority to automatically charge my card for anything.  But again, I'm told I have to call back.  I ask again about returning the machine - again, they tell me that department isn't open today because of covid, but when I call back when the payment posts, I can speak to them then.

Less than 1 week later, I get another charge, this time for $1,050!  I contacted Apria immediately.  They said the charge was for the purchase of the machine (what?!) that I'd been trying to return and that I'd never asked or agreed to purchase.  I explained the fact that I had been trying to return the machine, that I'd been getting charged for random amounts that were supposed to be refunded but haven't been, that they had no authority whatsoever to charge my card again after I paid the deposit.  It was a one time payment.  There was no mention of the possibility of additional charges.  I didn't even get a receipt, a statement, a notice - NOTHING.  As it's illegal to charge a debit card without consent, this is a very serious issue.  The representative tells me I signed up for automatic payments.  I told him I didn't and asked for proof - a verbal recording, a signature, or even a document sent with the machine.  He finally admitted there was no authority.  He admitted the payments should all be refunded.  But, then he says it will take at least 2 weeks because the payment hasn't posted in their system yet and that's how long it takes.  I said no, not good enough.  Too much money at stake.  I asked for a supervisor, but of course, they weren't available and would have to call me back in 2 or 3 business days.  Nope - I've heard that before from this company and I know it's a lie.  Oh, and I STILL don't know how to return the machine.  I asked AGAIN, but they ignored me.  One thing the representative said that really has me concerned is that there's another payment processing in their system for $1,150!!  So, they'll have taken over $2,100 from me without consent, authority or even notice.  All the while, they haven't let me return the machine.

I've submitted a complaint to the CA Department if Insurance, the BBB, and will be contacting Apria's corporate counsel (I am an attorney so I'm hoping I can get this resolved with him).  I've disputed the charges with my bank and had to cancel my debit card to ensure they don't charge me again.  After reading everyone else's experience, it seems to me that this company is scamming people out of money on a regular basis.  They've definitely done that in my case.  I hope people see these reviews before they ever get involved with Apria.< /text>

This is not a good review.  After seven or eight years of continual problems with Apria which included delivering wrong items, outright lies, and uncaring staff, my wife and I are at our wits end.  First, all calls to customer service or an attempt to reach a particular branch will connect you with someone in the Philippines.  You will never speak to anyone local.  Although they identify themselves as "Customer Care", they are anything but.  Hard to understand and most times unable to understand any simple concept you attempt to convey, their staff provide care by either confusing the issue or passing the buck back to you for you to solve "online".  The local branches are no better.  To wit:  After suffering an injury, my wife needed a specific commode as directed by her doctor.  Also, she needed it immediately.  Since it wasn't covered by our insurance, I agreed to pay cash.  After an hour on the phone with Apria customer care searching for the item at my insistence given the situation, they finally located one about 25 miles from my home at an Apria facility, but could not confirm that it was actually there.  I convinced them that I needed to call the branch myself to confirm and avoid an unnecessary trip.  They reluctantly gave me the number, I called the branch, gave them the brand and part number, the branch employee told me he was holding the item in his hand and, yes, it was the part number I was looking for.  I drove to the branch in SoCal afternoon traffic, walked in the door and they brought out a commode that was not only the incorrect part number, but did not resemble the item I needed by any stretch of the imagination.  They had no explanation for the error, even after swearing that they had what I needed.  It was late in the day, I was 25 miles from home and computer and had no idea how I was going to be able to help my wife.  This was customer service?  But today was the last straw.  My wife's rolling walker broke beyond repair unexpectedly two days ago on Wednesday.  Since using it was the only way she could get out of bed and move around the house, she requested and received a STAT approval for a replacement from her doctor and our insurance.  However, she needs a specific model which Apria had provided in the past on at least two occasions. He said that all he could do was return it and have the supervisor call me immediately.  When the supervisor called I explained the situation and the need for my wife to get a walker STAT. And the people that we have had contact with don't seem to care at all.  Unfortunately, you cannot contact anyone about the poor service (even the supervisors in customer care stonewall) and our health plan only contracts with them.  I would recommend that you avoid doing business with Apria.</review>

<Review>I have had Bell Pest Control Service since I purchased my first home in 2014. I recently purchased a new home in February and within the first month I had a large ant infestation in my home after an ant nest was disturbed following yard work that was done before I purchased the home. I haven't had to do any work in the yard yet, so it wasn't me:-) I called the office first thing in the morning hoping someone could come that day before the ants made it into my pantry. I wish I could remember the name of who I spoke with. She was absolutely lovely, sympathetic and went above and beyond to get techs to my house that afternoon. If I recall, she mentioned that she lives in Galt, I hope that helps her supervisor identify her.
Osmand and Isiah arrived that afternoon to spray inside and out, inspected my attic to make sure there were no rodents (as the home inspection noted some old droppings up there) and they inspected the backyard to see where the ants were coming from. Sure enough, Isiah was able to identify the source and followed the ant trail clear across my backyard to my fruit trees. They treated the area and walked me through everything they did before leaving. We set up a follow-up appointment for Osmand to return two-weeks later to check on the bait he placed in the attic and check on the ant situation.
At our follow-up appointment I informed Osmand that I thought there may be a dead rodent in my wall and I had been smelling it since the day I moved in, he also smelt it. He went straight to the attic, checked the old bait and placed an odor absorption bag in my attic to help with the odor as he couldn't find the animal. OMG it has only been an hour and the smell is already improving. He treated the backyard again as there was still a decent ant trail moving along my patio, but luckily no more ants in the house!! WOOHOO
In my opinion, Bell Pest Control is great. I have always lucked out getting truly amazing techs that seem to go above and beyond. They are always so professional, personable and genuine.
